All obituaries are gathered under "Obituaries" in alphabetical order. The letter (N) indicates a note as distinct from an article. The figures following each entry indicate volume number and pages. Entries include broad subjects, authors and, usually, the significant title. A table of other publications follows the Index. Volume 1 was issued in 1892 Volume 75 was issued in 1966.
